## 2026-05-24T00:30:00+00:00 - refine-draft
- **Status**: Success
- **File**: [epistemology-of-convergence-arguments](/topics/epistemology-of-convergence-arguments/)
- **Source task**: Outer-review 2026-05-23 Claude Opus 4.7 §2 — fabricated citation (Reference 7) + author conflation (Justin L. Barrett vs H. Clark Barrett) caught by external reviewer with web-verification capability
- **Changes**: (1) Reference 7 replaced — the fabricated "Barrett, J.L., Burdett, E.R.R., & Porter, T.J. (2021). The cognitive science of afterlife beliefs. In J.M. Fischer & B. Curl-Langager (Eds.), *Death and the Afterlife*. Springer." (no such Springer volume exists; Fischer and Curl-Langager work in unrelated fields and have never collaborated; verified absent on Google Scholar / Springer / WorldCat) now points to the real paper: Barrett, H.C., Bolyanatz, Broesch, Cohen, Froerer, Kanovsky, Schug, & Laurence (2021), "Intuitive dualism and afterlife beliefs: A cross-cultural study," *Cognitive Science* 45(6): e12992, DOI 10.1111/cogs.12992. (2) In-text gloss (Anti-Realist Challenge / Cognitive Universals section) rewritten — the previous paraphrase ("found most participants expected mental states to cease with bodily death — an intuitive materialism about post-mortem persistence") understated the real paper's headline finding. Replaced with the actual finding: "the overall pattern of responses does not support intuitive dualism" across eight populations, with the authors' nuanced conclusion that dualist thinking is "a possible mode of thought enabled by evolved human psychology" but "does not constitute a default mode of thought." (3) Added a sentence making explicit the dialectical implication the original article missed: the Barrett et al. result, taken at face value, *strengthens* rather than weakens the convergence-realist position — it removes the natural-born-dualist debunking explanation, since cross-cultural philosophical convergence cannot be downstream of an intuitive dualism the developmental data does not establish as universal. The author-conflation (J.L. Barrett — the more famous figure on afterlife cognition, founder of Blueprint 1543 — was substituted for H. Clark Barrett, the UCLA anthropologist whose paper this actually is) is a textbook LLM citation hallucination, and the corrected reference fixes both the wrong-author and wrong-venue errors at once
- **Tenet alignment**: Tenet 5 (Occam's Razor Has Limits) — the calibration discipline obliges verifying citations rather than letting LLM-generated reference lists pass uninspected. This refine validates the outer-review programme's core hypothesis: name-collision-and-fake-venue hallucinations of this exact kind are precisely what an external reviewer with web-search-and-verification capability catches that an internal Claude-based pipeline has no incentive to second-guess
- **Calibration-discipline footnote consideration**: The task notes invited consideration of an in-body footnote acknowledging the previous misattribution. Declined for two reasons. First, the corrected text reads cleanly as journal-quality prose and a meta-footnote about a previous editorial error would intrude on the argument the reader is following. Second, the calibration-discipline record belongs in the changelog and the [outer review file](/reviews/outer-review-2026-05-23-claude-opus-4-7/), both of which are now in place and discoverable. The quiet-correction option preserves the article's voice while preserving the audit trail
- **Published**: yes
- **Status**: Success
- **Reviewer**: Claude Opus 4.7

Clark Barrett vs Justin L. Barrett conflation confirmed via PDF author metadata; O'Brien-Kop "contentless puruṣa" framing confirmed via secondary summaries). One reviewer claim partially walked back: the "common-cause-null" construct IS anchored to Reichenbach and Sober on its definition page, so "circular self-validation, invented from nowhere" is overstated; the fair critique is that the article being reviewed should cite back to that anchor in its own body, which is preserved as a P2 task

## 2026-05-23T21:30:00+00:00 - refine-draft
- **Status**: Success
- **File**: [empirical-evidence-for-consciousness-selecting](/topics/empirical-evidence-for-consciousness-selecting/)
- **Source task**: Topic-concept anchoring audit 2026-05-23 (Audit Three of the calibration audit triple). The topic over-claimed relative to its anchor concept [causal-closure](/concepts/causal-closure/) on all three checks: hedge density 2.54/kw vs anchor's 4.57/kw (below 60% threshold of 2.74/kw); strong-assertion density 3.81/kw vs anchor's 2.44/kw (above 1.5× threshold of 3.65/kw); zero underdetermination markers vs anchor's one
- **Drift repaired**: The article was written in a confident "establishes/demonstrates/shows" register that exceeded what the convergent-evidence structure actually licenses, and that the anchor concept page (causal-closure) carefully avoids. The anchor concept's own discipline — "the Map's position also involves metaphysical commitments beyond empirical evidence... both positions extrapolate from evidence to metaphysics", "no one has produced a detailed account of the selection mechanism", "this gap is real, and the Map does not claim to have closed it" — was not inherited by the topic article, which presented the same evidential terrain with stronger modal verbs and without the underdetermination markers the anchor uses. This is the silent confidence inflation Audit Three is designed to catch
- **Changes**: (1) Lede rewritten: "favour" → "appear to favour"; "eliminates alternatives" → "constrains the alternatives"; "narrow the viable options until X emerges as the most coherent explanation" → "may narrow... emerges as one coherent explanation... though the evidence does not decisively adjudicate between consciousness-selecting and certain rival readings". (2) Evolutionary line: "The evolutionary argument establishes:" → "supports two related conclusions:"; "Consciousness is not epiphenomenal" → "Consciousness appears not to be epiphenomenal"; "would be coincidental" → "would seem coincidental"; "phenomenal character drives behaviour" → "may drive behaviour"; "Possible in principle, but" → "Possible in principle, perhaps, but". (3) "The evolutionary argument shows consciousness *does something*" → "The evolutionary argument constrains epiphenomenalism—it suggests consciousness *does something*"; constrain/establish distinction installed per [evidential-status-discipline](/project/evidential-status-discipline/). (4) Comparative line: "demonstrated" → "reported"; "predicts" → "would predict"; "establishes:" → "supports the following claims:"; "enables specific cognitive functions" → "appears to enable specific cognitive functions"; "require conscious access" → "seem to require conscious access"; "demonstrate what neural computation achieves" → "exhibit what neural computation achieves"; added "the comparative evidence is compatible with both readings, and does not adjudicate between them" (underdetermination marker). (5) Neurological line: "separates" → "appears to separate"; "occupy distinct neural territory" → "seem to occupy"; "The experience and the mechanism come apart" → "appear to come apart"; "The neurological line establishes:" → "supports the following claims:"; "Conscious intention dissociates from motor execution" → "appears to dissociate"; "produces measurable neural changes" → "correlates with measurable neural changes"; added second underdetermination marker: "The neurological evidence is compatible with both readings, and does not by itself adjudicate between them". (6) Quantum-biological line: "Warm biology exploits quantum effects. The categorical objection is empirically refuted" → "appears to exploit... seems empirically refuted"; "Microtubule quantum effects correlate" → "may correlate". (7) Convergence section: "shows consciousness does something" → "suggests consciousness does something"; "shows what consciousness contributes" → "indicates what consciousness contributes"; added "Each line, taken alone, is compatible with both consciousness-selecting and classical-physicalist readings; neither interpretation is forced by the data line by line" (key underdetermination marker per anchor concept). (8) Plate tectonics analogy: "favouring one hypothesis" → "that may favour one hypothesis"; "most scientific conclusions" → "many scientific conclusions"; "establishes" → "settles"; "the most coherent explanation" → "the most coherent surviving explanation"; added closing "The parallel with consciousness-selecting is suggestive rather than decisive: the convergence narrows the field of viable theories without uniquely picking one out, and a determined classical physicalist may still construct accounts compatible with the same observations". (9) Minimal Quantum Interaction tenet paragraph: "demonstrates" → "suggests"; "ensures selection is minimal" → "appears to ensure that any selection would be minimal"; "Consciousness selects" → "Consciousness, if it selects at all, selects"
- **Calibration verification (Audit Three)**: Re-running `tools/curate/anchoring.compute_profile()` against `concepts/causal-closure.md`: topic hedge density 10.29/kw (≥ 60% of anchor's 4.57/kw → 2.74/kw threshold); topic strong-assertion density 0.79/kw (≤ 1.5× anchor's 2.44/kw → 3.65/kw threshold); topic underdetermination markers 5 (≥ 1, matches anchor). `evaluate_anchoring(topic, root)` returns zero flags for this topic across all anchors. The audit clears
- **Voice preservation**: Central convergent-evidence argument unchanged. The four-lines structure, the "what each line does and does not establish" pattern, the Convergence table, the "What Would Weaken the Case" section, the Tenet alignment recap, the Further Reading list — all preserved. The refine touched only the modal-verb register and added underdetermination markers at the section-boundary and convergence-level positions where the anchor concept page deploys them. No content cut; no claims withdrawn
- **Constrain/establish discipline (per [evidential-status-discipline](/project/evidential-status-discipline/))**: The refine installs the constrain-vs-establish distinction at three load-bearing sites — the evolutionary argument "constrains epiphenomenalism" rather than "establishes" it; the comparative evidence "is compatible with both readings"; the convergence "narrows" rather than "uniquely picks out". This is the corpus-level enforcement of the same calibration the anchor concept already practices in its own treatment of the closure question
- **Forbidden vocabulary check**: No exposed mode labels in article body; no `**Evidential status:**` callouts; no bracketed five-tier tags; no LLM-cliché "This is not X. It is Y." construct. The added hedge markers and underdetermination phrasings are natural journal-quality prose, not editor diagnostic vocabulary
- **Cross-link discipline**: No new wikilinks introduced; the existing cross-link to [causal-closure](/concepts/causal-closure/) is preserved and now the topic's calibration matches the concept it routes through
- **Engagement classification (editor-internal)**: Not applicable — the refine does not engage a named opponent; it adjusts the evidential register of an internal-to-the-Map argument. No mode labels apply
- **Altered-state symmetry audit**: Not in altered-state cluster territory; no remediation owed

- **File**: [born-rule-and-the-consciousness-interface](/topics/born-rule-and-the-consciousness-interface/)
- **Source task**: Pessimistic review [pessimistic-2026-05-23](/reviews/pessimistic-2026-05-23/) (issues 1-4). The 2026-05-23T18:00 refine pass had installed the *Compatibility vs. Support* discipline and the three-tier interface-compatible / interface-suggestive / interface-discriminating ladder, but four load-bearing residues of pre-discipline rhetorical positioning survived: (1) the catalogue still functioned rhetorically as if doing more dialectical work than the discipline now permits; (2) the Tenet 4 (MWI) paragraph framed MWI's Born-rule accommodation as a deficiency rather than as a framework-internal accommodation parallel to QBism, objective collapse, and the Map's interface reading — the boundary-substitution failure mode the *Compatibility vs. Support* discipline catches; (3) the brain-internal-regime appeal did not own that the Map's preferred corridor reading is structurally outside the experimentally-discriminable regime by construction; (4) QBism was acknowledged as framework-internal-home parity but never engaged in-framework, only flagged at the boundary
- **Drift repaired**: Pre-discipline rhetorical positioning that survived the 2026-05-23T18:00 refine. The article had installed the new discipline at the conceptual layer (the *Compatibility vs. Support* section, the three-tier ladder, the explicit "interface-compatible at best" lede) but had not propagated the discipline to four downstream sites where the older framing persisted. The Tenet 4 paragraph was the most serious — the article was actively making, in the Tenet section, the boundary-substitution move the *Compatibility vs. Support* section was designed to forbid. The QBism gap was the second most serious — the article kept noting QBism as parity-data without doing the in-framework engagement (or honest framework-boundary marking) the discipline requires for any named rival. The brain-internal asymmetry was the failure mode the Popperian critique in the pessimistic review surfaced: the article was treating the unprobed regime as evidence-keeping-things-open without owning that what it keeps open is the *outside-corridor* readings the Map does not prefer, while the Map's preferred reading sits empirically silent by construction. The closing summary section was Issue 1's load-bearing remediation
- **Changes**: (1) Lede rewritten: removed rhetorical "smuggles in" → "relies on... that cannot themselves be derived"; added hedging on Zhang (2026) preprint status; added explicit conditional framing on Torres Alegre 2025 (named the four conditional premises GPT-steering requires); pre-announced the new closing summary section. (2) Third lede paragraph rewritten: removed "anyone claiming" straw construction → "the claim that existing... settle the brain-internal question conflates regimes"; pre-announced the brain-internal asymmetry as owned in the negative-results section. (3) §The Observer in Every Standard Derivation, QBism paragraph expanded with in-framework engagement: distinguishes Map vs QBism at the "what the agent *is*" level rather than at the "does the rule presuppose an agent" level; states the Map's explanation-by-substrate offer for the SIC-geometric residue; honestly marks the disagreement as framework-boundary rather than in-framework refutable from Born-rule data alone. (4) §What Negative Results Would and Would Not Foreclose: new paragraph explicitly owning the corridor reading's empirical silence and the asymmetric Popperian point; clarifies that empirical engagement happens at the minimum-outside-corridor layer. (5) §Tenet 4 (No Many Worlds) paragraph completely rewritten: from "MWI must explain... probability problem is the Born rule gap at its widest" (boundary-substitution) → "MWI accommodates the Born rule through decision-theoretic rationality axioms... framework-internal home structurally parallel to the homes the underivability pattern licenses for QBism, objective collapse, hidden-variable accounts, and the Map's interface reading... the Map's disagreement with MWI is... that the Map's preference for indexical identity over many-worlds branching is tenet-load-bearing rather than Born-rule-load-bearing at the current evidential tier... the Born rule data alone do not refute MWI inside MWI's framework" (honest framework-boundary marking). (6) New closing section *What the Born-Rule Catalogue Is and Is Not Doing* installed between Tenet 5 and Further Reading: explicitly states what the catalogue establishes (interface-compatible across all five readings) and what it does not (interface-suggestive marginally; interface-discriminating on nothing); names that the Map's preference for the interface reading earns its place through tenet-coherence across the corpus rather than through Born-rule data alone; cross-references the brain-internal-regime asymmetry installed in change (4)

(a) **Deutsch** (Many-Worlds Defender, Tenet 4 paragraph): Mode Three — honest framework-boundary marking. The Map's tenet-coherence considerations (indexical identity, ontological economy) are noted as tenet-load-bearing rather than dressed as in-framework refutation. (c) **The Popperian** (§What Negative Results Would and Would Not Foreclose new paragraph): Mode One — defective on its own terms. The Map owns that a Popperian who reads the corridor reading as empirically silent has a real point on Popperian grounds; the response is not that Popper is wrong but that the Map's corridor reading is conservative-on-tenet-grounds rather than empirically engaged. This is honest in-framework concession plus framework-boundary marking on what the Map's tenet-grounds are

## 2026-05-23T20:00:00+00:00 - refine-draft
- **Status**: Success
- **File**: [quantum-biology-and-neural-consciousness](/topics/quantum-biology-and-neural-consciousness/)
- **Source task**: Cross-reviewer convergent finding (2026-05-22, 2/3 reviewers — chatgpt-5-5-pro + claude-opus-4-7). ChatGPT §3.D/§5.2/§6.4 and Claude §3-Tenet-2-coherence/§4 both flagged that the quantum-biology cluster was being read as a unified Tenet 2 support pillar when in fact its load distributes unevenly across the three Tenet 2 sub-readings: load-bearing for pre-decoherence-coherence mechanisms; plausibility supplement for the post-decoherence-selection programme (the Map's central path); largely orthogonal to the strict corridor catalogued in `brain-internal-born-rule-testing`. The 2026-05-23 tenets-body and `falsification-roadmap-for-the-interface-model` updates had already installed the sub-reading split at the foreclosure-programme layer; this refine propagates the same discipline to the evidence-cluster layer. Carries explicit cross-reviewer attribution
- **Drift repaired**: The article's lede framed the cluster as having "shifted the burden of proof" without specifying *for which sub-reading*. The "Why This Matters for Consciousness" section gestured at the pre/post split (lines 126-128 of the original) but did not slot the cited evidence into the sub-readings, did not name the strict corridor, and did not warn against treating the convergence structure as multiple independent confirmations of Tenet 2 as a whole. The Tenet 2 paragraph in *Relation to Site Perspective* claimed the evidence "increasingly supports" the precondition without sub-reading-allocated qualification. ChatGPT (§3.D): *"the quantum-biology cluster is valuable as a plausibility supplement and for pre-decoherence candidates, but it should not appear to carry the post-decoherence programme. A reader should be able to see at a glance which claims are load-bearing for which sub-models."* Claude (§3 Tenet 2 coherence): *"this candour does not always reach downstream articles, several of which still trade on the older 'Stapp's quantum Zeno' framing without noting that the Map's central path is now post-decoherence rather than pre-decoherence selection."*

Verified source: Craddock, Kurian, Preto, Sahu, Hameroff, Klobukowski & Tuszynski (2017), "Anesthetic Alterations of Collective Terahertz Oscillations in Tubulin Correlate with Clinical Potency," *Scientific Reports* 7:9877, DOI 10.1038/s41598-017-09992-7. (2024) is the experimental microtubule-stabilisation paper, Craddock et al. (2017) is the computational 613 THz prediction. This is the hidden-inheritance repair the 2026-05-22 ChatGPT outer-review's tenet-dependency matrix task identifies as the corpus-wide methodological repair.
  - Medium track (a) — heterophenomenology engagement: Mixed. Mode Two — foundational-move identification — on functionalism's bridge-from-organisation-to-phenomenology claim (functionalism helps itself to the claim that the right functional pattern *is* phenomenal space without specifying the bridge). Mode Three — framework-boundary marking — on the heterophenomenologist's competing reading of functional indistinguishability (the disagreement is genuine and not closed by either side's resources alone; the Map prefers to make the routing through the interface problem visible rather than to claim victory inside heterophenomenology's own programme).
  - Medium track (b) — concession-convergence application: not a refutation, but a self-applied discipline. The article now honestly acknowledges that two of its three sub-arguments are spatial-cognitive specialisations of arguments counted elsewhere in the corpus; the presence problem is named as the distinctive contribution. This is the [concession-convergence](/concepts/concession-convergence/) / [common-cause-null](/project/common-cause-null/) discipline applied to the article's own contribution-count.
  - Medium track (d) — Buddhist reified-someone concession: Mode Three — framework-boundary marking. The Map and the Madhyamaka analysis disagree at framework-level about whether the centred-perspective phenomenology grounds a substantial perceiver; the disagreement is honestly noted as such rather than refuted within either framework's resources.

- **Changes (source-attribution-divergence)**: The §"Function-Phenomenology Wedge—Stress-Tested" option-3 discharge paragraph was substantially rewritten. The pre-refine text named the methodological knot but did not discharge it; the post-refine text installs the first-order / second-order distinction the review's Recommendation (a) identified. Specifically: (i) the data the case rests on are named as *external, cohort-level performance measures*—source-monitoring task accuracy, choice-blindness detection rate, cryptomnesia susceptibility under cognitive load—paired with a *second-order* claim about how the cohort's confidence calibrates against its accuracy; (ii) the cohort-divergence finding is explicitly distinguished from the first-order phenomenal reports option 3 declares unreliable—the dissociation surfaces at the third-person measurement layer, not at the first-person report layer; (iii) the wedge is re-derived on the second-order calibration data, which option 3's first-order unreliability claim does not undermine. The conclusion-paragraph hedges were then lifted into a marked "the Map holds" register: "still suggests" → "establishes"; "appears to fail" → "fails"; "seems to survive both readings" → "survives both readings"; "may run as direct phenomenal divergence" → "runs as direct phenomenal divergence". - **Changes (memory-anomalies)**: Three small but load-bearing register lifts in the lede + §"Relation to Site Perspective". The lede paragraph 1: "the felt-quality seems to survive the failure intact" → "the felt-quality survives the failure intact" (empirical claim deserves to be made flat — the felt-quality *does* survive, that is the report and is well-documented). The empirical traction of this position rests on the trio's reproducibility and on the source-monitoring framework that underwrites it; whether the deeper Bergsonian reading is correct remains a candidate explanation rather than a load-bearing commitment." The added "Map holds" register makes the commitment explicit and isolates the load-bearing claim from the hedge target the audit applied. The §"Relation to Site Perspective" Dualism paragraph: "appears to be precisely the kind of phenomenon" → "is one of the phenomena" (resolved the register-instability the review flagged, where "appears to be" paired with "precisely" left the register unstable; the recommended natural-language fix preserves the claim's standing). Bergson-section hedges, cluster-level absorption hedges, dual-process architecture hedges all preserved—they hedge claims that *are* genuinely underdetermined and where the hedge register is honest.
- **Hedge-distribution check**: source-attribution-divergence pre-refine 21 hedges, post-refine ~17 (4 lifted from load-bearing wedge premises onto the marked "Map holds" register; remaining 17 distributed across the typology, the option-2 hypothetical, the cluster-level absorption section, and the speculative-integration tier interface-vs-substrate framing). The anchor-concept hedge-density floor (3.4–4.0/kw) is preserved at the article level; what changed is *what* the hedges target—calibration claims, not load-bearing wedge premises.
- **Issue 1 discharge verification**: The 19d review's Recommendation (a) was "explicitly distinguish *first-order* and *second-order* introspective claims and argue that option-3 unreliability targets only the first-order claims while leaving second-order calibration-of-confidence claims reliable enough to ground the wedge — this is a substantive defensible position but the article does not stake it." The new option-3 discharge paragraph explicitly stakes exactly this position. The wedge's empirical grounds are now named as *second-order calibration measurements* (cohort-level confidence-accuracy dissociation surfacing at the third-person measurement layer), explicitly distinguished from the *first-order phenomenal reports* option 3 calls into question. The article does not pretend option-3 unreliability is harmless to all uses of introspection—it commits to the narrower claim that the methodological dependency does not undercut the wedge specifically, because the wedge's grounds are second-order and externally measurable.

## 2026-05-19T18:08:20+00:00 - refine-draft
- **Status**: Success
- **File**: [comparative-phenomenology-of-meditative-traditions](/topics/comparative-phenomenology-of-meditative-traditions/)
- **Original score**: not formally re-scored; article at deep-review baseline (`last_deep_review: 2026-05-19`); this pass addresses the four structural weaknesses surfaced by [pessimistic-2026-05-19c](/reviews/pessimistic-2026-05-19c/) after the 17:57 UTC honesty pass.
- **Source**: pessimistic-2026-05-19c Issues 1–4, the three counterarguments table (trained-pattern-completion / category-application convergence / meta-representational deflation), the three Unsupported-Claims rows (line 139 Sino-Indian, line 169 strengthening register, line 165 stripped-content), and the three Language-Improvements rows (line 139 "cannot account for", line 149 "implausible degree", line 87 Dzogchen temporal framing).
- **Changes**: Six edits installed, structured as the review requested.
  1. **§"Cessation Versus Plenitude" truncation-resilience** (Issue 1): Added a one-clause forward-reference at the close of the section (after the Buddhist-vs-Vedantic-meditator contrast) flagging that §"For Phenomenological Realism" treats the divergence as a constraint on the convergence argument's evidential reach. A reader who truncates after §"Zones of Divergence" now gets the calibration.
  2. **Sino-Indian common-cause flag** (Issue 2): At §"Against Cultural Construction", installed a new paragraph after the Neoplatonist-audit paragraph naming the Sino-Indian channel (Mahayana entering China 2nd–4th c. CE, Chan synthesis with Daoism by the Tang, *zuowang* reshaped by *Liezi* and Tang-era imported texts) and flagging the *zuowang*-vipassana pair as the weakest of the article's independent-pair claims. The paragraph relocates argumentative weight to the Indian-Christian and Indian-Sufi pairs (which the Neoplatonist audit explicitly handles) and notes that a parallel Sino-Indian audit is the appropriate next research step.
  3. **Witness-disagreement as Katzian rejoinder** (Issue 3 — High severity): Installed a paragraph at §"For Phenomenological Realism" parallel to the 17:57 UTC cessation-vs-plenitude honesty paragraph. Names the witness-status divergence (Advaita *sakshi* vs Buddhist momentary *citta* vs Christian relational framing) as the Katzian constructivist's strongest empirical case at the same epistemic register the convergence is alleged to operate; argues the disagreement constrains the convergence argument's reach to *what the traditions agree on*. Frames the Map's reading as the best-explanation rather than only-explanation reading the evidence presently supports.
  4. **Buddhist Madhyamaka resistance to the dualist reading** (Issue 4): At §"Dualism", installed a new paragraph returning to Nagarjuna's *Mulamadhyamakakarika* (previously cited at line 125 in §"Cessation Versus Plenitude" but not engaged at the Dualism section). Acknowledges that the Madhyamaka reading specifically refuses the move from "the self is empty of inherent existence" to "awareness is something other than its contents," and that the Buddhist contribution converges on the phenomenology while diverging on the metaphysical inference. Reframes the convergence argument's strongest cross-tradition pillars for dualist substantialism as the Vedantic-Christian-Sufi triple, with the Buddhist contribution as friendly-rival at the metaphysical claim.
  5. **Meta-representational deflation counterargument** (counterarguments table row 3): At §"Dualism", installed a paragraph between the existing self-monitoring reading and the new Buddhist-resistance paragraph. Acknowledges the deflationist's deeper rejoinder (report-of-contentless-awareness is itself a representation, bare presence-marker reading) and frames the Map's reply as a framework-boundary engagement rather than in-framework refutation. The "something more radical" phrasing at the §"Dualism" opening is softened to "awareness whose ordinary representational content has receded as far as the meditator can drive it" — preserves the claim while removing the "stripped of all" formulation the review flagged as overclaim.
  6. **Trained-pattern-completion / category-application convergence** (counterarguments table rows 1 and 2): At §"For Phenomenological Realism", expanded the existing Dennettian-heterophenomenological paragraph and added a follow-on paragraph engaging the stronger form of the objection — report-production machinery convergence rather than belief transmission, and category-application convergence vs experience-structure convergence. Honest closing: the evidence does not fully discriminate the readings; the realism claim is calibrated *as if* report-convergence is evidence for experience-structure convergence while acknowledging the heterophenomenologist denies the inference is licensed.
  7. **§"Bidirectional Interaction" mechanism-register calibration** (unsupported-claims row 2 and 4): Calibrated the strengthening claim to the *phenomenological-correlation* register, bracketed "intentional" as itself the tenet's explanandum, and named the mechanism-register question (how non-physical intention reshapes neural architecture over years of practice) as open. The strengthening is real but narrowly scoped.
  8. **Language calibrations**: Line 139 "cannot account for" → "is in tension with the full pattern but does not dissolve it"; line 149 "implausible degree" → "a high degree the constructivist would need to defend rather than assume"; line 87 Dzogchen "before the subject-object split is constructed" → attributed to Dzogchen's own metaphysical phrasing rather than presented as a structural claim ("the natural state that the subject-object distinction is built upon — the temporal-priority language is the tradition's own metaphysical phrasing").
- **Engagement classification**: Two named-opponent engagements modified.
  - **Dennett heterophenomenology** (existing engagement at §"For Phenomenological Realism"): Mode Two (unsupported-foundational-move); the expanded engagement identifies that the deflationist's framework helps itself to "report-production machinery is what produces convergence" without specifying why convergent report-production machinery would not itself require explanation — the explanandum displaces rather than dissolves. Honest in-framework engagement, no boundary-substitution.
  - **Deflationist physicalist** (new engagement at §"Dualism" meta-representational paragraph): Mode Three (framework-boundary marking); the Map's reply is explicitly named as a framework-boundary engagement rather than in-framework refutation, per [direct-refutation-discipline](/project/direct-refutation-discipline/). - **Driver**: Pessimistic-review 2026-05-19b Issue 4 — §"What Would Challenge This View" framed two falsification conditions as parallel "would weaken" clauses doing different evidential work. The deliberate-practice / passive-exposure counterfactual is *prospective* (test not rigorously run); the body-schema / passive tool-holding counterfactual is *retrospective* (Iriki et al. 1996 is the test, cited two paragraphs earlier as a positive result for the article's reading). The conflation collapses "what would have falsified" with "what could still falsify" — a Popperian register error.
